#### MOUNTAIN ORCS AND GUNDABAD #####						
#####################################						
#####################################

### History ###

# JUKE NOTE: MOST OF THIS IS HEAVILY OUTDATED AND NO LONGER REFLECTS REALMS LORE.
# Most notably, The Gundabad orcs NO LONGER all descend from eachother and Azog is born in Moria much later, instead of being an angmar orc

### Second Age ###
# Skorg conquers Gundabad and his direct line holds it up the war of the last alliance. After that Durin V reconquer Gundabad and Skorgs linage splits apart to smaller houses. 

### Third age ###
# The spawn(Urro, Aarlok & Orkarmur) of Grimtok, the last ruler of Gundabad before Dwarves retook it, escapes and survive the loss of Gundabad and form might factions from the survivng orc forces of Gundabad.
# Urro forms the Lokikrah-kai (Dragon claw) and his factions rebuilds it strengh somewhere around the mountains of withering heath, they retake gundabad sometime around 350 T.A. 
# Aarlok form's a dynasty that spreads Skorgs blood in forodwaith, while Orkarmur does the same but joins up and forms Uruk-Ongmair (orcs of Angmar) later on
# the Lokikrah-kai builds a power base in the grey mountains where they convert to dragon cult and then around 350-450 t.a. attacks and retakes gundabad
# 
# 1267 T.A. A  Balcog emerges from either Ered Mithrin or forodwaith. Wishing to restore the cult of Ulûkai he'd amassed a great number of orcish warriors (and supported by the Nazgûl-lord on his quest to found the realm of Angmar) he attacks Mount Gundabad in force during the summer but is unable to take it immediately
# 1268-1280 T.A. The Nazgûl-lord is able to array his forces for the final stroke against any opposition in his realm-to-be. The dwarven fortress of Barazbizar (Carn Dûm) is taken 12741. Secretly, the orcish king at Mount Gundabad is made an ally of Angmar with the establishment of that realm
# 1268-1974 T.A. Mount Gundabad serves as the principal orcish citadel in the Hithaeglir. Gundabad’s strength is used extensively by the Witchking in his wars against the successor realms of Arnor. At first this is done covertly, but beginning in the mid-19th century, also more openly.
# T.A. 1975 T.A. Angmar falls, Gundabad is no longer a pupet under Angmar, and gain some of it's forces that belonged to the eastern Angmar borders. The line of Trupalog-kai can not hold the kingdom of gundabad togather and it falls apart into duchies.

# 2055 T.A. Azog the defiler conquers Gundabad from Trupalog-kai orcs, and restores the Kingdom of Gundabad whom de jure land both have the Worauthai Madur & Uruk Ongmair cultured orcs in it, he unifies them into the Ghrazim, the Rack-Horde (in orcish), Gundabad Orcs
# 2793-2799 T.A. War of the Dwarves and Orcs, end's with the death of Azog
# 2799 T.A  Bolg takes over up to the point of 2941 T.A. when the Battle of the five armies 2941, where he perishes 
# 2941 T.A Gorgol first son of Bolg, flees back to Gundabad and assumes control, with his forces weakened and with the shock of the loss of his father he fears he can not complete the Ulûkai quest, so dosn't immidetly assume the Ashdurbúk quest, which his Brother Gorgar view as weakness and plans to usurp him

### Worauthai Madur ###
# The Northerners or Free Tribes of the North
## In order:
# Line of Skorg, the first decendents of Skrog. While the other dynasties would also identiyfy and claim to be of his decendence this is the first line before them splitting
# Line of Urro, Grimtok's spawn. after the war of the las alliance Grimtok lose gundabad to Durin V and his heirs split and form new houses. Urro's line goes to thw withered heath. [made-up by Rémerod]
# Line of Aarlok, Grimtok's spawn. after the war of the las alliance Grimtok lose gundabad to Durin V and his heirs split and form new houses. Aarlok escapes to forofwaith [made-up by Rémerod]
# Line of Orkarmur, Grimtok's spawn. after the war of the las alliance Grimtok lose gundabad to Durin V and his heirs split and form new houses. Orkarmur escapes to forofwaith and later are one of the ones that forms Uruk-Ongmair [made-up by Rémerod]
# Line of Balcog of the Gurhoi-hai, an ofshoot of the Bolgdur-hai, retakes Gundabad from the Lokikrah-kai and restores the Cult of the Ulûkai

### Uruk Ongmair ###
# The Orcs of Angmar (Or.Uruk-Ongmair) originally were a coalition of Orc Tribes from the northern Misty mountains and the surrounding lands which had been pressed into the service of the Witch-King of Angmar.
## In order
# Line of Bakzur of the Durbalag, One of Radzag spawns, breaks apart the Bolgdur-hai and his fathers realm along with his siblings 
# Line of Trupalog, the Trupalog(-kai) one of the tribes of the [Uruk-Ongmair/Orcs of Angmar](https://notionclubarchives.fandom.com/wiki/Orcs_of_Angmar)
# Line of Thrakburzum, lords of Mount Gram

### Ghrazim ###
# Ghrazim, the Rack-Horde (in orcish), Gundabad Orcs
## In Order
# Line of Azog The Defiler! One of the greatest orc since the time of Skorg, founder of the house Ashmog, given to Azog when he visited the Necromanzer before taking Gundabad (made up by Rémerod)

### Orcs of Mirkwood - WIP
# Maghaz Family - TOR Character - Captain of Dol Guldur's Orc Garrison in Mirkwood
# Other Characters

#### Angmar Start Date - Lines overview ####

## Angmar proper (k_angmar) ##
# Line of Ghruzshul ~ High Chieftains of Mt. Gram
# Line of Rikkarr ~ holding the remaining counties in the Mt Gram duchy
# Line of Muzdug ~ Minor Chieftains in Nan Angmar under the Witch-king's control
# Line of Krimpbar ~ Minor Chieftains in Nan Angmar under the Witch-king's control
# Line of Tozrakh ~ Minor Chieftains in Nan Angmar under the Witch-king's control
# Line of Yargrak ~ High Chieftains of Foryagsh, vassals of Angmar
# Line of Forthrokh ~ Minor chieftains in the duchy of Foryagsh
# Line of Hizgur ~ Minor chieftains in the duchy of Foryagsh
# Line of Zorgratak ~ Minor chieftains in the duchy of Foryagsh 
# Line of Burzlukh ~ Minor chieftains in the duchy of Foryagsh
# Line of Durzugh ~ Minor chieftains in the duchy of Foryagsh
# Line of Oshrakazh ~ Minor chieftains in the duchy of Kalenemas

## Misty Mountains (e_misty_mountains) ##
# Line of Korglub ~ Minor unbound Orcs in Gunduz Mahab
# Line of Worgrakh ~ Minor unbound Orcs in Gunduz Mahab
# Line of Firrakh ~ Orc Chieftains of Pass of Gundabad, under the Witch-king
# Line of Rugdukh ~ Orc Chieftains of Gundalok, vassals of Angmar
# Line of Pugrakh ~ Orc Chieftains of Ugulai, Vassals of Angmar
# Line of Úgrog ~ Orcs in the deepest depths of the southern Misties
# Line of Kur Razhûr ~ Orcs in the deepest depths of the southern Misties

## Greenwood (e_greenwood) ##
# Line of Balgrúkh ~ Minor Chieftains in the Mts. of Mirkwood
# Line of Grozablokh ~ High Chieftains of Taurannon and Nidurn
# Line of Húgrkah ~ Chieftains of Gorodrod under the Necromancer 
# Line of Rothrúkh ~ Chieftains of Dimbar under the Necromancer
# Line of Borkagh ~ Chiefains of Barad Angol under the Necromancer
# Line of Norbog ~ Chieftains of Naerorn under the Necromancer

## Grey Mountains (k_grey_mountains) ##
# Line of Grumlókh ~ High Chieftains of the Withered Heath
# Line of Hakrog ~ Minor vassal Chieftains of Nor-dûm
# Line of Rorak ~ Minor vassal Chieftains of Usmek
# Line of Molug ~ Minor vassal Chieftains of the Vale of Drakes
# Line of Bukrog ~ Orcs that at one time attempted to settle the Rhûn Mountains
